        <script>
         const isMobileRegex = /Android|BlackBerry|iPhone|iPad|iPod|Opera Mini|IEMobile|WPDesktop/i;
                const checkMobile = () => navigator.userAgent.match(isMobileRegex);
                const getOSType = () => {
                  let OSName = "unknown-os";
                  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Win") !== -1) {
                    OSName = "windows-os";
                  }
                  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Mac") !== -1) {
                    OSName = "mac-os";
                  }
                  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("X11") !== -1) {
                    OSName = "unix";
                  }
                  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Linux") !== -1) {
                    OSName = "linux";
                  }
                  return OSName;
                }
                if ((!checkMobile() || window.innerWidth > 767) || getOSType() != 'windows-os') {
                  // Load the IFrame Player API code asynchronously.
                  var videoPlayer;
                  var player, timer;
                  var time_update_interval;
                  // Replace the 'ytplayer' element with an <iframe> and
                  // YouTube player after the API code downloads.
                                      Object.defineProperty(HTMLMediaElement.prototype, 'playing', {
                      get: function() {
                        return !!(this.currentTime > 0 && !this.paused && !this.ended && this.readyState > 2);
                      }
                    });
                    videoPlayer = document.querySelector('#video_player');
                    initialize();
                                  }

                function initialize() {
                  updateTimerDisplay();
                  clearInterval(time_update_interval);
                  time_update_interval = setInterval(function() {
                    updateTimerDisplay();
                  }, 1000)
                }

                function isYouTubePlaying() {
                  if (
                    document
                    .querySelector(".header-wrapper")
                    .classList.contains("animate-header")
                  ) {
                    clearInterval(timer);
                    document
                      .querySelector(".animating-parent")
                      .classList.add("animateSubHeading1");
                  }
                }

                function updateTimerDisplay() {
                  const gameLogo = document.querySelector('.game-logo');
                  if (!checkMobile() && getOSType() != 'windows-os') {
                    if (!videoPlayer && !player) {
                      setTimeout(() => {
                        document.querySelector('.animation-wrapper').classList.add('next-step');
                        document.querySelector('.animation-wrapper').style.opacity = 0;
                        document.querySelector('.header-wrapper').classList.add('animate-header');
                        document.querySelector('.bg-img').classList.add('removeFilter');
                        if (gameLogo) {
                          gameLogo.classList.remove('hide');
                        }
                        let heroWindows = document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section-win.hide');
                        if (heroWindows) {
                          document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section-mac').style.background = "linear-gradient(45deg,rgba(0,0,0,.4),rgba(0,0,0,.2),rgba(0,0,0,.4)), url('https://cdn-www.bluestacks.com/takeovercms-prod/2020-05-19/SOS-EN-wb.jpg') fixed center / cover no-repeat";
                        } else {
                          document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section').style.background = "linear-gradient(45deg,rgba(0,0,0,.4),rgba(0,0,0,.2),rgba(0,0,0,.4)), url('https://cdn-www.bluestacks.com/takeovercms-prod/2020-05-19/SOS-EN-wb.jpg') fixed center / cover no-repeat";
                        }
                        timer = setInterval(isYouTubePlaying, 1000);
                      }, 3000);
                    } else {
                      if (videoPlayer) {
                        videoPlayer.style.opacity = 1;
                      } else if (player) {
                        document.querySelector('.animation-wrapper iframe').style.opacity = 1;
                      }
                      if (player && player.getCurrentTime() > '8') {
                        player.pauseVideo();
                      } else if (videoPlayer && videoPlayer.currentTime > '8') {
                        videoPlayer.pause();
                      }
                      if ((player && player.getCurrentTime() > '4') || (videoPlayer && videoPlayer.currentTime > '4')) {
                        let heroWindows = document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section-win.hide');
                        if (heroWindows) {
                          document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section-mac').style.background = "linear-gradient(45deg,rgba(0,0,0,.4),rgba(0,0,0,.2),rgba(0,0,0,.4)), url('https://cdn-www.bluestacks.com/takeovercms-prod/2020-05-19/SOS-EN-wb.jpg') fixed center / cover no-repeat";
                        } else {
                          document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section').style.background = "linear-gradient(45deg,rgba(0,0,0,.4),rgba(0,0,0,.2),rgba(0,0,0,.4)), url('https://cdn-www.bluestacks.com/takeovercms-prod/2020-05-19/SOS-EN-wb.jpg') fixed center / cover no-repeat";
                        }
                        document.querySelector('.animation-wrapper').style.opacity = 0;
                        document.querySelector('.animation-wrapper').classList.add('next-step');
                        document.querySelector('.header-wrapper').classList.add('animate-header');
                        document.querySelector('.bg-img').classList.add('removeFilter');
                        if (gameLogo) {
                          gameLogo.classList.remove('hide');
                        }
                        clearInterval(time_update_interval);
                      }
                    }
                  } else {
                    if (player) {
                      player.pauseVideo();
                    }
                    if (videoPlayer) {
                      videoPlayer.pause();
                    }
                  }
                }

                if (getOSType() != 'windows-os') {
                  const macSection = document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section-mac');
                  const winSection = document.querySelector('.hero-banner-section-win');
                  if (macSection && winSection) {
                    macSection.classList.remove('hide');
                    winSection.classList.add('hide');
                  }
                }
